name:R‚Äçi‚Äçc‚Äçh‚Äçt‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Twin Room
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Couples
info:4 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 10, 2024
msg:The place to stay in Tianjin!  We always stay here when returning to Tianjin.  Location is the best and service is outstanding.   Take Metro Line 1 - Exit XiaoBaiLou station and go out the A or D exit.  A is shorter but D exit has less stairs (if you are pulling luggage).   As you exit you will see the hotel directly in front of you.    Rooms are of a classic design with solid walls ensuring a good sleep.  Windows can be opened which is a nice feature.   Staff are all very helpful, friendly and enthusiastic.  There are many shops, restaurants, parks and other attractions all within walking distance or short metro ride.   We did not have the hotel breakfast this time but on prior visits it has been fantastic.   Tianjin is well known for great breakfasts - do not miss the Jianbing guozi !     Thank you to everyone at the Clarion for making our stay so enjoyable.   We hope to be back soon.

msg:I had to attend an appointment here at short notice, so I drove to Tianjin with my boyfriend. It was too late and I didn't want to go back to Beijing. Let me comment on this hotel objectively.
Location: First of all, it is very convenient to take a taxi or bus. It is located in the central area. Next to it is the famous Cheeseland.
There are also many food around, and there are stalls at night.
Parking: It is very inconvenient. The hotel does not have its own parking lot. Only 20 cars can be parked at the door. There is an underground parking lot opposite, but it takes a long way to walk up. The weather is very hot. It is easier to park at the Friendship Hotel next to it.
Facilities: Old hotel, very old, it should be a good hotel in the 1970s and 1980s. But now it seems very inconvenient, and it is obviously not upgraded. The shower, charging port, and air conditioning are not very easy to use, especially the air conditioning, it is so hot. . . It is not cool even after opening for a whole day.
Service: Give 5 points. The hotel called me to inquire about the check-in situation. I said that you don‚Äôt have a USB charging port, and you charge it with a charge. The hotel immediately sent someone to deliver the plug. But I just want to ask, why not equip the room with a charging head instead of a charge? Such good service is given to the front desk, but not to the hotel itself.
Hygiene: As an old hotel, I trust the hygiene conditions, but to be honest, the bathroom should be cleaned.

There is a delicious breakfast stand next to the hotel, recommended.
